The car is a seven-seater business car and is very spacious. The driver drives very steadily. On the way, he also introduced us to the customs and customs of Suqian.
Goodnight porridge for two: The porridge and side dishes are very good. The child was hungry at more than ten o'clock in the evening, and drank all two bowls of red dates and rice porridge.
Facilities: The room is very large. The child looks here and there. There are super large floor-to-ceiling windows and the scenery outside is very good. The 2-meter big bed is super big, and the child is not crowded at all when sleeping between us. The bathing facilities are also great, the bathtub is very large, and the smart toilet is also well received.
Service: The service is the most commendable. When you arrive at the hotel entrance, there is a handsome doorman brother to open the car door to help with the luggage. There are beautiful girls who help pull the suitcase throughout the hotel. The housekeeper gave the child a puzzle toy, and the room also thoughtfully prepared fruits and milk, as well as towels folded into bunnies. When checking out, I gave my child a toy car, a yo-yo and a big rocket piggy bank, which he liked very much. He told me directly that he would stay in this hotel again next time he went out to play, and it seemed that he was really satisfied.
